<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
const URL_METEOROLOGIA = "https://blogdolago.com.br/category/geral/meteorologia/";

function irParaMeteorologia(event) {
    // Redireciona apenas se não clicar no botão de fechar
    window.location.href = URL_METEOROLOGIA;
}

function fecharAlerta(event) {
    event.stopPropagation(); // Impede que o clique no botão ative o link da barra
    const barra = document.getElementById('barra-alerta-sti');
    barra.style.display = 'none';
    document.body.style.marginTop = "0px";
    sessionStorage.setItem('alerta_clima_fechado', 'true');
}

(function() {
    const checarClima = async () => {
        if (sessionStorage.getItem('alerta_clima_fechado')) return;

        const barra = document.getElementById('barra-alerta-sti');
        const msg = document.getElementById('texto-alerta');
        
        try {
            const url = "https://api.open-meteo.com/v1/forecast?latitude=-25.43&longitude=-54.40&current_weather=true&daily=precipitation_probability_max&timezone=America/Sao_Paulo";
            const response = await fetch(url);
            const data = await response.json();
            
            const temp = Math.round(data.current_weather.temperature);
            const code = data.current_weather.weathercode;
            const probChuva = data.daily.precipitation_probability_max[0];
            
            let ativo = false;

            if ([95, 96, 99].includes(code)) {
                msg.innerHTML = "⛈️ ALERTA CRÍTICO: Tempestade em STI. Clique para detalhes e precauções.";
                barra.style.background = "#b91c1c"; 
                ativo = true;
            } 
            else if (temp >= 36) {
                msg.innerHTML = `🔥 CALOR EXTREMO: STI com ${temp}°C. Veja as recomendações na nossa página de meteorologia.`;
                barra.style.background = "#ea580c"; 
                ativo = true;
            }
            else if (probChuva > 60) {
                msg.innerHTML = `🌧️ PREVISÃO DE CHUVA: ${probChuva}% de probabilidade para hoje em STI. Leia mais.`;
                barra.style.background = "#1d4ed8"; 
                ativo = true;
            }

            if (ativo) {
                barra.style.display = 'block';
                document.body.style.marginTop = barra.offsetHeight + "px";
            }
        } catch (e) { console.error("Erro no alerta."); }
    };

    window.addEventListener("load", checarClima);
})();
</script>

					<p>Aprenda a otimizar seu Outlook no celular com dicas práticas para Android e iPhone. Organize e gerencie seus e-mails de forma profissional e eficiente. Clique e confira!</p>

height: auto;" decoding="async" srcset="https://blogdolago.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/a4614fd1-cb49-41e0-937c-bde54ee2d6d1.png 1024w, https://blogdolago.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/a4614fd1-cb49-41e0-937c-bde54ee2d6d1-300x300.png 300w, https://blogdolago.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/a4614fd1-cb49-41e0-937c-bde54ee2d6d1-150x150.png 150w, https://blogdolago.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/a4614fd1-cb49-41e0-937c-bde54ee2d6d1-768x768.png 768w, https://blogdolago.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/a4614fd1-cb49-41e0-937c-bde54ee2d6d1-120x120.png 120w, https://blogdolago.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/a4614fd1-cb49-41e0-937c-bde54ee2d6d1-96x96.png 96w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></noscript></a></div><div id="text-3" class="col-md-12 widget widget_text">			<div class="textwidget"><div id="clima-sti-final" style="min-height: 120px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; font-family: sans-serif; color: #666;">
    <span>⏳ Carregando clima...</span>
</div>

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
(function() {
    const atualizarClima = async () => {
        const box = document.getElementById('clima-sti-final');
        if (!box) return;

        try {
            // Chamada para a API
            const response = await fetch("https://api.open-meteo.com/v1/forecast?latitude=-25.43&longitude=-54.40&current_weather=true&daily=temperature_2m_max,temperature_2m_min&timezone=America/Sao_Paulo");
            
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Erro na rede');
            
            const data = await response.json();
            const temp = Math.round(data.current_weather.temperature);
            const code = data.current_weather.weathercode;
            const max  = Math.round(data.daily.temperature_2m_max[0]);
            const min  = Math.round(data.daily.temperature_2m_min[0]);

            // Definição de Ícones
            let icon = "☀️"; let desc = "Céu Limpo";
            if ([1, 2, 3].includes(code)) { icon = "🌤️"; desc = "Nublado"; }
            else if ([45, 48].includes(code)) { icon = "🌫️"; desc = "Neblina"; }
            else if ([51, 53, 55, 61, 63, 65, 80, 81, 82].includes(code)) { icon = "🌧️"; desc = "Chuva"; }
            else if ([95, 96, 99].includes(code)) { icon = "⛈️"; desc = "Tempestade"; }

            // Insere o visual final
            box.innerHTML = `
                <div style="background: #fff; border: 1px solid #e2e8f0; border-radius: 12px; padding: 15px; text-align: center; width: 100%; max-width: 200px; box-shadow: 0 4px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.05);">
                    <div style="font-size: 10px; color: #94a3b8; text-transform: uppercase; font-weight: 700; margin-bottom: 8px;">Santa Terezinha de Itaipu</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 38px; margin-bottom: 5px;">${icon}</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 32px; font-weight: 800; color: #1e293b; line-height: 1;">${temp}°C</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 13px; color: #64748b; margin-top: 8px;">${desc}</div>
                    <div style="display: flex; justify-content: center; gap: 12px; margin-top: 12px; padding-top: 10px; border-top: 1px solid #f1f5f9; font-weight: bold;">
                        <span style="color: #ef4444;">↑ ${max}°</span>
                        <span style="color: #3b82f6;">↓ ${min}°</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        } catch (error) {
            box.innerHTML = "<small style='color:#ccc;'>Clima indisponível</small>";
            console.error("Erro ao buscar clima:", error);
        }
    };

    // Garante que o script rode mesmo se o site for lento
    if (document.readyState === "complete") {
        atualizarClima();
    } else {
        window.addEventListener("load", atualizarClima);
    }
})();
</script>

</select>
</form><script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript">
/* <![CDATA[ */

( ( dropdownId ) => {
	const dropdown = document.getElementById( dropdownId );
	function onSelectChange() {
		setTimeout( () => {
			if ( 'escape' === dropdown.dataset.lastkey ) {
				return;
			}
			if ( dropdown.value && parseInt( dropdown.value ) > 0 && dropdown instanceof HTMLSelectElement ) {
				dropdown.parentElement.submit();
			}
		}, 250 );
	}
	function onKeyUp( event ) {
		if ( 'Escape' === event.key ) {
			dropdown.dataset.lastkey = 'escape';
		} else {
			delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
		}
	}
	function onClick() {
		delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
	}
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'keyup', onKeyUp );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'click', onClick );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'change', onSelectChange );
})( "cat" );

//# sourceURL=WP_Widget_Categories%3A%3Awidget
/* ]]> */
</script>
